							}

								OR = {
									has_trait = wrathful

					}

							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.438.g #Good that we have modern medical equipment.
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = triage
		}
		add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
		custom_tooltip = dubois_triage_tt
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.438.h #We wait until they recover
		sub_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
	}

	after = {
	}
}

#Dubois 439: Rope Group

dubois.439 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.439.t
	desc = dubois.439.d
	flavor = dubois.439.f

	placement = scope:dubois_summit_location

	duration = 3

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_mountaineering_climb.dds"
	}

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		years = 1
	}

	trigger = {
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 5
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress > 1
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.433.g #Go ahead
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = opium_addiction
									has_trait = senile
									has_trait = wounded
									has_trait = psychological_affliction
								}
							}
						}
						add = 15
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = wrathful
									has_trait = hedonist
									has_trait = plains_commander
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 65
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								age >= 75
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				trigger_event = { 
					id = dubois.421 #Dangerous Fail
					popup = yes
				}
			}
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = surveyor
							}
						}
						add = 5
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_modifier = dubois_aspiring_climber_modifier
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = cautious
									has_trait = meticulous
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = brave
									has_trait = innovative
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								OR = {
									has_trait = ambitious
									has_trait = persistent
								}
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = explorer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = mountain_commander
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							scope:dubois_mountain_expedition_leader = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 20
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
							scope:dubois_mountain_scientist = {
								has_trait = dubois_mountaineer
							}
						}
						add = 10
					}
				}
				add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.438.g #Good that we have modern organization.
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			has_technology_researched = logistics
		}
		add_dubois_mountain_climbing_progress = yes #Success
		custom_tooltip = dubois_logistics_tt
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.431.h #This is too risky
	}

	after = {
	}
}

	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_geology.dds"

	cooldown = {
		days = 100
	}

	trigger = {
		exists = scope:dubois_mountain_scientist
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.440.g #Congratulations
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
				var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
					has_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var
				}
			}
			dubois_add_x_specimen_effect = { AMOUNT = 1000 }
			naturalist_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = "5"
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
				var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
					has_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var
				}
			}
			dubois_add_1_fossil = yes
			paleontologist_experience_gain_effect = {
				AMOUNT = "5"
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

		years = 100
	}

	trigger = {

		has_variable = dubois_naturalist_var
		var:dubois_naturalist_var = {
			has_variable = dubois_mountain_scientist_var
		}
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress <= 4
		var:dubois_mountain_climbing_progress > 1
	}

	immediate = {
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_leader_effect = yes
		set_dubois_summit_location = yes
		set_dubois_mountain_expedition_scientist_effect = yes
	}

	option = {

		custom_tooltip = dubois_zoo_animal_transport_tt
		add_modifier = {
			name = dubois_zoo_transport_modifier
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.148
				days = { 30 60 }
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
	}
}

				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1013.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1013.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			desc = dubois.1013.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

    event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_zoo_afr_lions.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_role = general
				is_busy = no
				age >= 70
			}
			save_scope_as = dubois_prinz_eugen
		}
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			0 = { 
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_scope_character = {
								has_role = general
								is_busy = no
								age >= 70
							}
							NOT = {
								has_variable = dubois_prinz_eugen_var
							}
						}
						add = 70
					}
				}
				set_variable = dubois_prinz_eugen_var
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1012.k #Return to the African Enclosures
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			scope:dubois_prinz_eugen = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_eugen_and_the_lion_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_african_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1011
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			scope:dubois_prinz_eugen = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_eugen_and_the_lion_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			scope:dubois_prinz_eugen = {
				kill_character = yes
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_eugen_and_the_lion_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_lion_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1036: Platypus Enclosure
dubois.1036 = {
	type = country_event

    title = dubois.1036.t
    desc = dubois.1036.d
    flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.1036.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1036.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1036.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
				}
			}
			desc = dubois.1036.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

    event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_animal_platypus.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			8 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			8 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			8 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			1 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1032.k #Return to the Australian and Oceanian 
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
					has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_australian_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1031
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
					has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
				}
				AND = {
					has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
					has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
				}
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_platypus_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1032.g #A Platypus? Perry the Platypus!
		trigger = {
			has_variable = dubois_perry_the_platypus_var
			NOT = {
				has_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
			}
		}
		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.1036
			popup = yes
		}
		set_variable = dubois_perry_left_var
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_dubois_zoo
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_unknown_hero_modifier
				years = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1043: Eurasian Wolf Enclosure
dubois.1043 = {
	type = country_event

    title = dubois.1043.t
    desc = dubois.1043.d
    flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.1043.f1
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1043.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1043.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			desc = dubois.1043.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

    event_image = {
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_animal_wolf.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

    duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			10 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			10 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			10 = {
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			0 = { 
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_modifier = elgar_prokofiev_great_composer_modifier
								any_scope_state = {
									has_modifier = elgar_prokofiev_performance_modifier
								}
							}
							NOT = {
								has_variable = dubois_prokofiev_and_the_wolf_var
							}
						}
						add = 70
					}
				}
				set_variable = dubois_prokofiev_and_the_wolf_var
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_wolf_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

								has_pop_culture = greek
							}
							NOT = {
								country_has_primary_culture = cu:greek
							}
							NOT = {
								has_variable = dubois_new_hercules_var
							}
						}
						add = 70
					}
				}
				set_variable = dubois_new_hercules_var
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1052.k #Return to the North American Enclosures
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_north_american_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1051
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_new_hercules_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					is_capital = yes
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_new_hercules_modifier
					years = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_grizzly_flavor_randomizer_var

dubois.1055 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1055.t
	desc = dubois.1055.d
	flavor = {

			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 1
			}
			desc = dubois.1055.f1
		}

			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 2
			}
			desc = dubois.1055.f2
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 3
			}
			desc = dubois.1055.f3
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			desc = dubois.1055.f4
		}
	}

	placement = root

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_animal_panther.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_character = {
			limit = {
				has_trait = literary
			}
			save_scope_as = manzoni_literary_scope
		}
		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 2
				}
			}
			10 = { 
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 3
				}
			}
			0 = { 
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_scope_character = {
								has_trait = literary
							}
							NOT = {
								has_variable = dubois_the_panther_var
							}
						}
						add = 70
					}
				}
				set_variable = dubois_the_panther_var
				set_variable = {
					name = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
					value = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1052.k #Return to the North American Enclosures
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_north_american_enclosures_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1051
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_the_panther_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.l #Return to the Main Entrance
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = zoo_main_entrance_tt
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.1001
				popup = yes
			}
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var = 4
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_the_panther_modifier
				years = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1001.m #Leave the Zoo
		default_option = yes
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = leave_zoo_tt
			remove_variable = dubois_visiting_zoo_var
			remove_variable = dubois_zoo_panther_flavor_randomizer_var

#Animal Babies

#Dubois.1101: A Baby animal was born
dubois.1101 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1101.t
	desc = dubois.1101.d
	flavor = dubois.1101.f

	placement = root

	event_image = { #Lion Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 1
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_lion.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Otter Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 2
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_otter.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Jaguar Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 3
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_jaguar.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Koala Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 4
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_koala.dds"
	}

	event_image = { #Panda Baby
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 5
		}
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/zoo_babies/dubois_baby_panda.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/middleeast/jungle_expedition"
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	cooldown = {
		years = 25
	}

	trigger = {
		is_player = yes
		NOR = {
			has_modifier = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
			has_global_variable = dubois_no_more_baby_animals_global_var
		}
		any_scope_building = {
			is_building_type = building_dubois_zoo
			level > 0
		}
		OR = {
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_lion
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_otter
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_jaguar
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_koala
			has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_panda
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				has_building = building_dubois_zoo
			}
			save_scope_as = zoo_state_scope
		}

		random_list = { #randomizes flavor text
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_lion
				}
				set_variable = { #Lion
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 1
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_otter
				}
				set_variable = { #Otter
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 2
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_jaguar
				}
				set_variable = { #Jaguar
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 3
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_koala
				}
				set_variable = { #Koala
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 4
				}
			}
			1 = {
				trigger = {
					has_variable = dubois_zoo_animal_panda
				}
				set_variable = { #Panda
					name = dubois_zoo_baby_type
					value = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	###### Baby names ######
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 1 --> Bubbles
	### Lions ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 2 --> Simba (Lion)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 3 --> Zuri (Lion)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 4 --> Kya (Lion)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 5 --> Lwazi (Lion)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 6 --> Nala (Lion)
	### Otters ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 7 --> Otto (Otter)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 8 --> Oskar (Otter)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 9 --> Alice (Otter)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 10 --> Max (Otter)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 11 --> Freja (Otter)
	### Jaguar ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 12 --> Cihuacoatl  (Jaguar)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 13 --> Yaotl  (Jaguar)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 14 --> Feliz (Jaguar)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 15 --> Santiago (Jaguar)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 16 --> Isabella (Jaguar)
	### Koala ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 17 --> Alfie (Koala)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 18 --> Pippa (Koala)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 19 --> Uki (Koala)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 20 --> Milo (Koala)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 21 --> Victoria (Koala)
	### Panda ###
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 22 --> Meng Xiang (Panda)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 23 --> Xiao Qi Ji (Panda)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 24 --> Fu Ni (Panda)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 25 --> Po (Panda)
	# dubois_baby_animal_name = 26 --> Tao Tao (Panda)

	option = {
		name = dubois.1101.bubbles #Bubbles

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_baby_animal_name
			value = 1
		}
		
		scope:zoo_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1011.lion_name_1 #Simba (Lion)

		trigger = {
			var:dubois_zoo_baby_type = 1
		}

		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_baby_animal_name
			value = 2
		}

		scope:zoo_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_animal_baby_modifier
				months = 12
			}
		}
	}

######NATURE RESERVE######

#Dubois 1201: Nature Reserve Location found

dubois.1201 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1201.t
	desc = dubois.1201.d
	flavor =  dubois.1201.f

	placement = root

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_north_america.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		#triggered by dubois_nature_reserve_survey_decision 
	}

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
			value = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					dubois_state_has_mountains = yes
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					dubois_state_has_mountains = yes
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
				}
				save_scope_as = dubois_mountain_state_scope
			}
			set_local_variable = dubois_mountain_state_var
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					dubois_state_has_forest = yes
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOT = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					dubois_state_has_forest = yes
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOT = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = dubois_forest_state_scope
			}
			set_local_variable = dubois_forest_state_var
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					dubois_state_has_fjord = yes
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOT = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					dubois_state_has_fjord = yes
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOT = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = dubois_fjord_state_scope
			}
			set_local_variable = dubois_fjord_state_var
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					dubois_state_has_desert = yes
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					dubois_state_has_desert = yes
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = dubois_desert_state_scope
			}
			set_local_variable = dubois_desert_state_var
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_state = {
					has_state_trait = state_trait_lake_victoria
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_desert_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_trait = state_trait_lake_victoria
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_desert_state_scope
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = dubois_lake_victoria_state_scope
			}
			set_local_variable = dubois_lake_victoria_state_var
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var < 3
				any_scope_state = {
					count > 0
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_desert_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_lake_victoria_state_scope
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_desert_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_lake_victoria_state_scope
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = dubois_additional_state_1_scope
			}
			set_local_variable = dubois_additional_state_1_var
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var < 3
				any_scope_state = {
					count > 0
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_desert_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_lake_victoria_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_additional_state_1_scope
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_desert_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_lake_victoria_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_additional_state_1_scope
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = dubois_additional_state_2_scope
			}
			set_local_variable = dubois_additional_state_2_var
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var < 3
				any_scope_state = {
					count > 0
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_desert_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_lake_victoria_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_additional_state_1_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_additional_state_2_scope
					}
				}
			}
			random_scope_state = {
				limit = {
					arable_land > 0
					is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
					NOR = {
						this ?= scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_forest_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_desert_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_lake_victoria_state_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_additional_state_1_scope
						this ?= scope:dubois_additional_state_2_scope
					}
				}
				save_scope_as = dubois_additional_state_3_scope
			}
			set_local_variable = dubois_additional_state_3_var
			change_variable = {
				name = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
				add = 1
			}
		}
		remove_variable = dubois_number_of_nature_reserve_states_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1201.g #A state with mountains like [Scope] is ideal!
		trigger = {
			has_local_variable = dubois_mountain_state_var
		}

		scope:dubois_mountain_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_nature_reserve_location_modifier
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1201.h #The vast forests of [scope] will be perfect!
		trigger = {
			has_local_variable = dubois_forest_state_var
		}

		scope:dubois_forest_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_nature_reserve_location_modifier
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1201.i #The fjords of [scope] are ideal for a Nature Reserve!
		trigger = {
			has_local_variable = dubois_fjord_state_var
		}

		scope:dubois_fjord_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_nature_reserve_location_modifier
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1201.j #Who needs a desert anyways? It is perfect!
		trigger = {
			has_local_variable = dubois_desert_state_var
		}

		scope:dubois_desert_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_nature_reserve_location_modifier
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1201.k #Where else than Lake Victoria?
		trigger = {
			has_local_variable = dubois_lake_victoria_state_var
		}

		scope:dubois_lake_victoria_state_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_nature_reserve_location_modifier
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1201.l #[Scope] looks like a good place for a Nature Reserve!
		trigger = {
			has_local_variable = dubois_additional_state_1_var
		}

		scope:dubois_additional_state_1_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_nature_reserve_location_modifier
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1201.m #I like [Scope]!
		trigger = {
			has_local_variable = dubois_additional_state_2_var
		}

		scope:dubois_additional_state_2_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_nature_reserve_location_modifier
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1201.n #We have to choose [Scope]!
		trigger = {
			has_local_variable = dubois_additional_state_3_var
		}

		scope:dubois_additional_state_3_scope = {
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_nature_reserve_location_modifier
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1210: [Scope Animal] in [Scope State] is endangered

dubois.1210 = {
	type = state_event

	title = dubois.1210.t
	desc = dubois.1210.d
	flavor = dubois.1210.f

	placement = root

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_habitat_destruction.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1210.g #We have to protect those animals!
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = dubois_endangered_habitat_tt
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_habitat_endangered_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_habitat_endangered_timer_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = dubois_habitat_protection_path_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_habitat_protection_path_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_technology_researched = dubois_genetics_tech
					is_ai = yes
				}
				is_homeland_of_country_cultures = owner
				is_incorporated = yes
			}
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				trigger = { 
					owner = {
						ig:ig_intelligentsia = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ig:ig_rural_folks = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ig:ig_landowners = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ruler = {
							OR = {
								is_interest_group_type = ig_intelligentsia
								is_interest_group_type = ig_rural_folk
								is_interest_group_type = ig_landowners
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1210.h #Progres above everything else!
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = dubois_endangered_habitat_tt
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_habitat_endangered_modifier
			}
			add_modifier = {
				name = dubois_habitat_endangered_timer_modifier
				years = 10
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_modifier = dubois_habitat_destruction_path_modifier
					}
				}
				add_modifier = {
					name = dubois_habitat_destruction_path_modifier
					years = 5
				}
			}
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ig:ig_industrialists = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ig:ig_trade_unions = {
							is_in_government = yes
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
			modifier = {
				trigger = {
					owner = {
						ruler = {
							OR = {
								is_interest_group_type = ig_industrialists
								is_interest_group_type = ig_trade_unions
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add = 1000
			}
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 1250: Yosemite National Park

dubois.1250 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.1250.t
	desc = dubois.1250.d
	flavor = dubois.1250.f

	placement = scope:yosemite_state_scope

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_nature_reserve_yosemite.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_animals.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	duration = 3

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_variable = dubois_yosemite_event_var
		}
		year >= 1890
		has_technology_researched = dubois_genetics_tech
		OR = {
			this ?= c:USA
			this ?= c:CAL
			was_formed_from = USA
			was_formed_from = CAL
		}
		p:x0AF8FD = {
			owner = root
		}
		any_scope_state = {
			state_region = s:STATE_CALIFORNIA
			NOT = {
				has_building = building_dubois_national_park
			}
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		random_scope_state = {
			limit = {
				state_region = s:STATE_CALIFORNIA
			}
			save_scope_as = yosemite_state_scope
		}
		set_variable = dubois_yosemite_event_var
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1250.g #This is a great idea!
		
		scope:yosemite_state_scope = {
			start_building_construction = building_dubois_national_park
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = dubois.1250.h #Actually, this looks like a great place for mining!

		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

#Dubois 2001: Main

dubois.2001 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2001.t
	desc = dubois.2001.d

	flavor = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var 
			}
			desc = dubois.2001.f_paleontologist
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
				}
			}
			desc = dubois.2001.f_no_paleontologist
		}
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_paleontological_collection.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var 
			}
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit the Paleontologist
		name = dubois.2001.i
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_paleontologist = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2011
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit Special Fossils
		name = dubois.2001.j
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_special_fossil = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2021
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit Human Evolution
		name = dubois.2001.k
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_human_fossil = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2031
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit Dinosaur Bones
		name = dubois.2001.l
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_dinosaur_bone = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2041
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Visit Dinosaur Skeletons
		name = dubois.2001.m
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_dinosaur_skeleton = yes
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2051
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		default_option = yes
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}
}

		}

					has_modifier = dubois_paleontologist_travell_to_location_modifier
					has_modifier = dubois_paleontologist_travell_from_location_modifier
				}
				scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
					is_busy = yes
				}
			}
			desc = dubois.2011.d_other
		}
	}
	flavor = dubois.2011.f

	gui_window = event_window_1char_tabloid

	left_icon = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	trigger = {
	}

	immediate = {
		var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
			save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
		}
	}

	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt

#Dubois 2041: Dinosaur Bones

dubois.2041 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2041.t
	desc = dubois.2041.d

	flavor = dubois.2041.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_collection_dinosaur_bones.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var
			}
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Fossils to bone
		name = dubois.2041.g
		trigger = {
			dubois_has_transformable_dinosaur_bone = yes
			var:dubois_fossil >= 20
			exists = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = dubois_paleontologist_experienced
					has_trait = dubois_paleontologist_famous
				}
				is_busy = no
			}
		}
		dubois_fossils_for_transformation_effect = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
								var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 175
							}
						}
						add = 25
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
								var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 200
							}
						}
						add = 25
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
								var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 250
							}
						}
						add = 50
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
								var:dubois_paleontologist_experience >= 300
							}
						}
						add = 50
					}
				}
				trigger_event = {
					id = dubois.2042
					days = { 50 60 }
				}
			}
			50 = {
				trigger_event = {
					id = dubois.2043
					days = { 50 60 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct North American Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.h
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_north_american_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_ankylosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_diplodocus_var
				has_variable = dubois_triceratops_var
				has_variable = dubois_tyrannosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_stegosaurus_var
			}
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_north_american_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_north_american_dinosaur = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct South American Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.i
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_south_american_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_antarctosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_argyrosaurus_var
			}
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_south_american_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_south_american_dinosaur = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct European Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.j
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_european_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_iguanodon_var
				has_variable = dubois_plateosaurus_var
			}
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_european_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_european_dinosaur = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct African Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.k
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_african_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_giraffatitan_var
				#has_variable = dubois_melanorosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_spinosaurus_var
			}
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_african_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_african_dinosaur = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct Asian Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.l
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_asian_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_psittacosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_velociraptor_var
			}
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_asian_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_asian_dinosaur = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Construct Australian Dinosaur
		name = dubois.2041.m
		trigger = {
			var:dubois_australian_dinosaur_bone >= 5
			NAND = {
				has_variable = dubois_muttaburrasaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_rhoetosaurus_var
			}
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = dubois_construct_australian_dinosaur_var
		dubois_construct_dinosaur_effect = yes
		dubois_construct_australian_dinosaur = yes
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}
}

			}

		}
		triggered_desc = {

			}

		}

			}

		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {

			}
			desc = dubois.2051.argyrosaurus
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_iguanodon_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2051.iguanodon
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_plateosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2051.plateosaurus
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_giraffatitan_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2051.giraffatitan
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_spinosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2051.spinosaurus
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_psittacosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2051.psittacosaurus
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_velociraptor_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2051.velociraptor
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_muttaburrasaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2051.muttaburrasaurus
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_rhoetosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2051.rhoetosaurus
		}
	}

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_dinosaur_skeleton_overview.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	option = {	#North American Skeleton
		name = dubois.2051.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_variable = dubois_ankylosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_diplodocus_var
				has_variable = dubois_triceratops_var
				has_variable = dubois_tyrannosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_stegosaurus_var
			}
		}

			popup = yes

			}
		}

		trigger_event = {

			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#European Skeleton
		name = dubois.2051.i
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_variable = dubois_iguanodon_var
				has_variable = dubois_plateosaurus_var
			}
		}

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2131
			popup = yes
		}
	}

	option = {	#African Skeleton

#Dubois 2112: Ankylosaurus

dubois.2112 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2112.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_perfect_ankylosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_perfect_dinosaur
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_imperfect_ankylosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_imperfect_dinosaur
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_poor_ankylosaurus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_poor_dinosaur
		}
	}

	flavor = dubois.2112.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_dinosaur_skeleton.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var 
			}
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Remount Ankylosaurus
		name = dubois.2112.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_variable = dubois_imperfect_ankylosaurus_var
				has_variable = dubois_poor_ankylosaurus_var
			}
			exists = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		set_variable = dubois_remount_ankylosaurus_var
		dubois_remount_dinosaur_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to North America Section
		name = dubois.2112.h

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2111
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}

#Dubois 2113: Diplodocus

dubois.2113 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2113.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_perfect_diplodocus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_perfect_dinosaur
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_imperfect_diplodocus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_imperfect_dinosaur
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_poor_diplodocus_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_poor_dinosaur
		}
	}

	flavor = dubois.2113.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_dinosaur_skeleton.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var 
			}
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Remount
		name = dubois.2112.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_variable = dubois_imperfect_diplodocus_var
				has_variable = dubois_poor_diplodocus_var
			}
			exists = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		set_variable = dubois_remount_diplodocus_var
		dubois_remount_dinosaur_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to North America Section
		name = dubois.2112.h

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2111
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}
}

			exists = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		set_variable = dubois_remount_plateosaurus_var
		dubois_remount_dinosaur_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to Europe Section
		name = dubois.2132.h

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2131
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}

#Dubois 2142: Giraffatitan

dubois.2142 = {
	type = country_event

	title = dubois.2142.t
	desc = {
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_perfect_giraffatitan_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_perfect_dinosaur
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_imperfect_giraffatitan_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_imperfect_dinosaur
		}
		triggered_desc = {
			trigger = {
				has_variable = dubois_poor_giraffatitan_var
			}
			desc = dubois.2112.d_poor_dinosaur
		}
	}

	flavor = dubois.2142.f

	event_image = { 
		texture = "gfx/event_pictures/dubois_pictures/dubois_dinosaur_skeleton.dds"
	}

	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_fossil.dds"

	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = dubois_paleontologist_var 
			}
			var:dubois_paleontologist_var = {
				save_scope_as = dubois_paleontologist_scope
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Remount Giraffatitan
		name = dubois.2112.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_variable = dubois_imperfect_giraffatitan_var
				has_variable = dubois_poor_giraffatitan_var
			}
			exists = scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope
			scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
				is_busy = no
				NOT = {
					has_modifier = dubois_exhausted_paleontologist_modifier
				}
			}
		}
		scope:dubois_paleontologist_scope = {
			set_character_busy = yes
		}
		set_variable = dubois_remount_giraffatitan_var
		dubois_remount_dinosaur_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			trigger_event = {
				id = dubois.2001
				popup = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to Africa Section
		name = dubois.2142.h

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2141
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Return to the Main Hall
		name = dubois.2001.h
		default_option = yes

		trigger_event = {
			id = dubois.2001
			popup = yes
		}
	}
	option = {	#Leave the Fossil Collection
		name = dubois.2001.g
		remove_variable = dubois_visiting_fossils_var

		custom_tooltip = dubois_leave_fossils_tt
	}
}
